    '''Convert a date of yyyy-mm-dd format to dd-mm-yyyy format.'''
    date = date.split('-')
    date[2] = date[2].split('.')
    date[2] = date[2][0]
    date[2] = date[2][2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]

    '''Convert a date of yyyy-mm-dd format to dd-mm-yyyy format.'''
    date = date.split('-')
    date[2] = date[2].split('.')
    date[2] = date[2][0]
    date[2] = date[2][2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:2]
    date[2
